button.</li></ul><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSI5ODkiIGhlaWdodD0iOTI2IiB2aWV3Qm94PSIwIDAgOTg5IDkyNiI+PHJlY3Qgd2lkdGg9IjEwMCUiIGhlaWdodD0iMTAwJSIgc3R5bGU9ImZpbGw6I2NmZDRkYjtmaWxsLW9wYWNpdHk6IDAuMTsiLz48L3N2Zz4=" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="989" height="926" data-src="https://bigg-boss-vote.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bb19.jpg" alt="Bigg Boss 19" class="wp-image-3326" data-srcset="https://bigg-boss-vote.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bb19.jpg 989w, https://bigg-boss-vote.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bb19-300x281.jpg 300w, https://bigg-boss-vote.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/bb19-768x719.jpg 768w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 989px) 100vw, 989px" /></figure></div><p>Well, Bigg Boss 19 is going to start on 24 August 2025 at Jio Cinema and the most crucial part is <a href="https://bigg-boss-vote.com/" data-wpel-link="internal"><strong>Bigg Boss 19 Voting Online</strong></a>, if you would like to know Bigg Boss 19 voting poll, here in this article, we have discussed how to vote for your favorite contestants.</p><p>Recently the official news was out about <strong>Bigg Boss 19 contestants</strong>, and we have discussed many things in this article, just go through this article from the beginning.</p><p>For the first time, Jio Cinema has released all the Bigg Boss 19 contestants&#8217; first looks. Get ready to save your favorite contestants with voting.</p><p>The <a href="https://bigg-boss-vote.com/" data-wpel-link="internal"><strong>voting poll of Bigg Boss 19</strong></a> will be opened once the show premiered. You can watch this show for free on Jio Cinema.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading">Faq</h3><div data-schema-only="false" class="wp-block-aioseo-faq"><h3 class="aioseo-faq-block-question">When will bigg boss season 19 start?</h3><div class="aioseo-faq-block-answer"><p>Bigg boss 19 starts on <strong>August 24, 2025</strong>, airing on Colors TV and Jio Cinema App.</p></div></div><div data-schema-only="false" class="wp-block-aioseo-faq"><h3 class="aioseo-faq-block-question">Will Bigg Boss 19 come on TV?</h3><div class="aioseo-faq-block-answer"><p>Yes, Bigg boss season 19 will be airing on Television only on Colors TV from 10 p.m onwards. Salman Khan will perform Weekend-Ka-Vaar on weekends at 9 p.m.</p></div></div><div data-schema-only="false" class="wp-block-aioseo-faq"><h3 class="aioseo-faq-block-question">Will Bigg Boss 19 come on Jio Cinema or Voot?</h3><div class="aioseo-faq-block-answer"><p>Jio Cinema bought OTT Rights for Bigg Boss Season 19, obviously bigg boss 19 will be available on <strong>Jio Cinema App</strong>. Where you can watch episodes aswell as live with extra clips.</p></div></div><div data-schema-only="false" class="wp-block-aioseo-faq"><h3 class="aioseo-faq-block-question">How to Vote in Bigg boss 19?</h3><div class="aioseo-faq-block-answer"><p>BB19 Voting is officially held on <strong>Jio Cinema App</strong> or <strong>Jio Cinema Website</strong>. <a href="https://bigg-boss-vote.com/#jiocinema-voting" data-wpel-link="internal">Click here</a> for full voting process.</p></div></div><div data-schema-only="false" class="wp-block-aioseo-faq"><h3 class="aioseo-faq-block-question">Who is hosting Bigg Boss 19?</h3><div class="aioseo-faq-block-answer"><p>Bigg Boss 19 is hosted by <strong>Salman Khan</strong>. The show will feature singles and couples as contestants.</p></div></div><div data-schema-only="false" class="wp-block-aioseo-faq"><h3 class="aioseo-faq-block-question">Who runs Bigg Boss?</h3><div class="aioseo-faq-block-answer"><p>Bigg Boss is an Indian TV reality show based on Big Brother, a Dutch reality show.
